	cost = 6

	}

			name = industrial_bonus
			bonus = 1.0
			uses = 2
			category = industry
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_RESEARCH }
}

	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus YAL_establish_ordenstaat_flussland"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					RIV = { exists = yes }
				}
				RIV = {
					clr_country_flag = river_federation_founder
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
					clear_variable = annexed_riv_members
				}
				clear_global_event_target = RivFed
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				HLQ = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			annex_country = { target = HLQ }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				LNS = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			annex_country = { target = LNS }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				LSM = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			annex_country = { target = LSM }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				LSC = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			annex_country = { target = LSC }
		}
		release_puppet = RCT
		every_possible_country = {
			limit = {
				has_character = LSM_konrada_wavewing
			}
			LSM_konrada_wavewing = {
				set_nationality = RCT
			}
		}
		RCT = {
			RIV_leave_fed_no_ally = yes
			set_cosmetic_tag = RCT_ordenstaat
			hidden_effect = {
				#load_focus_tree = rivercity_ordenstaat
				load_focus_tree = generic_griffon_focus
				retire_country_leader = yes
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = YAL_RCT_fasc_party_long
				name = YAL_RCT_fasc_party
			}
			add_popularity = { 
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.5
			}
			LSM_konrada_wavewing = {
				promote_character = holy_order_n
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = NIM
					is_core_of = BAK
					is_core_of = FRE
					is_core_of = DMT
					is_core_of = DEP
					is_core_of = WIT
					is_core_of = LCT
					is_core_of = ZES
					is_core_of = OLV
					is_core_of = FIR
					is_core_of = FBK
					is_core_of = WAT
					is_core_of = NCH
					is_core_of = BAR
				}
				# Some Riverland Nations might get cores on states of these tags, but the Empire should not cede states that it can integrate, therefore exclude
				NOT = { 
					OR = {
						is_core_of = LUS
						is_core_of = GRY
						is_core_of = HLQ
						is_core_of = LNS
						is_core_of = LSM
						is_core_of = LSC
						is_core_of = GRU
						is_core_of = BRF
						is_core_of = GRW
					}
				}
			}

			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }

					remove_idea = YAL_technocrats_3_mil
					add_idea = YAL_technocrats_3_mil_fin
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = YAL_technocrats_3_tech
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = YAL_technocrats_3_tech
					add_idea = YAL_technocrats_3_tech_fin
				}
			}
			else = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = YAL_technocrats_3_mil_tech
					add_idea = YAL_technocrats_3_all
				}
			}
		}
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = {
			localization_key = YAL_if_completed_focus
			FOCUS = YAL_clawnes
		}

		custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
		show_ideas_tooltip = YAL_lord_meynard_clawnes
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = {
			localization_key = YAL_if_completed_focus
			FOCUS = YAL_hawk
		}

		show_ideas_tooltip = YAL_august_von_hawk
	}

shared_focus = {
	id = YAL_cyrusval_university
	icon = GFX_YAL_cyrusval_university
	x = 14
	y = 1
	offset = {
		x = -14
		y = 0
		trigger = {
			has_game_rule = {
				rule = obsolete_focus_branches_visibility
				option = HIDE
			}
			has_completed_focus = YAL_cyrusval_university
		}
	}
	relative_position_id = YAL_gather_the_council
	cost = 5.00
	available = {
		has_country_flag = YAL_cyrusval
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = YAL_gather_the_council
	}
	mutually_exclusive = {
		focus = YAL_bruma_and_gamia
		focus = YAL_central_universities
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 4000
	}
	allow_branch = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = obsolete_focus_branches_visibility
					option = HIDE
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_completed_focus = YAL_bruma_and_gamia
					has_completed_focus = YAL_central_universities
				}
			}
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus YAL_cyrusval_university"
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = YAL_worker_support
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = YAL_intellectual_support
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = YAL_military_support
			value = 0
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = YAL_societal_divide2
			add_idea = YAL_societal_divide1
		}
		add_ideas = YAL_brewing_revolution

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = YAL_theodor_nierenstein
			}
			remove_ideas = YAL_theodor_nierenstein
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character = YAL_theodor_nierenstein
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				retire_character = YAL_theodor_nierenstein
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				YAL_theodor_nierenstein = {
					set_nationality = SOL
				}
			}
		}

		country_event = { id = yale.13 days = 7 }
		hidden_effect = { #collapse focus tree
			load_focus_tree = {
				tree = yale_focus
				keep_completed = yes
			}
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_MANPOWER FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = YAL_protect_the_ponies
	icon = GFX_goal_reach_out_vartai_angy
	x = 0
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = YAL_fight_racism
	cost = 5.00
	prerequisite = {
		focus = YAL_fight_racism
	}
	bypass = {
		LSC = { OR = { exists = no is_subject_of = ROOT has_war_with = ROOT } }
		LNS = { OR = { exists = no is_subject_of = ROOT has_war_with = ROOT } }
		LSM = { OR = { exists = no is_subject_of = ROOT has_war_with = ROOT } }
		event_target:longsword = { OR = { exists = no is_subject_of = ROOT has_war_with = ROOT } }
		HLQ = { OR = { exists = no is_subject_of = ROOT has_war_with = ROOT } }
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 40
	}
	will_lead_to_war_with = LSC
	will_lead_to_war_with = LNS
	will_lead_to_war_with = LSM
	will_lead_to_war_with = HLQ
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus YAL_protect_the_ponies"
		if = {
			limit = {
				LSC = { exists = yes NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT } }
			}
			LSC = { country_event = { id = yale.115 days = 3 } }
		} else_if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:longsword = { has_government = communism NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT } }
			}
			event_target:longsword = { country_event = { id = yale.115 days = 3 } }
		} else = {
			create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = event_target:longsword }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				LNS = { exists = yes }
			}
			create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = LNS }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				LSM = { exists = yes }
			}
			create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = LNS }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				HLQ = {
					OR = {
						owns_state = 552
						owns_state = 505
						owns_state = 540
					}
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = HLQ }
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
}

			}
		}

				is_owned_by_ROOT_or_ally = yes
			}

		YAL_anarchist_low_or_higher = yes
		YAL_syndie_low_or_higher = yes
	}

		factor = 40
	}

			target = HLQ

		}
		LSC = {
			every_core_state = {
				transfer_state_to = HLQ
			}
		}
		LSM = {
			every_core_state = {
				transfer_state_to = HLQ
			}
		}
		LNS = {
			every_core_state = {
				transfer_state_to = HLQ
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_MANPOWER FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL FOCUS_FILTER_WAR_SUPPORT FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY }
}

				value = 0.25
			}

				name = secret_bonus
				bonus = 0.5
				uses = 1
				category = nuclear
			}
		}
	}
